           <h1 name="fdc5" id="fdc5" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading graf--title">Build a “Serverless” Twilio SMS + Call Forwarding Bot in 7 Minutes using Node.js +&nbsp;StdLib</h1>
           <p name="3bb9" id="3bb9" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Since 2009, <a href="https://twilio.com/" data-href="https://twilio.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Twilio</a> has enabled developers to seamlessly build SMS and Voice technology into their apps, handling everything from basic user notifications, connecting drivers and passengers in apps like Uber and Lyft, to conference calling and more. If you haven’t had a chance to incorporate Twilio’s services into your product yet, here’s your chance to start! We’re happy to team up with Twilio’s functionality to show you how to bring Voice + SMS into your product or company in only a couple of minutes with StdLib!</p>
           <figure name="e62b" id="e62b" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 600px; max-height: 400px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 66.7%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*DRxMoUVu1SXHL6BCpR8xpQ.jpeg" data-width="600" data-height="400" data-is-featured="true">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*DRxMoUVu1SXHL6BCpR8xpQ.jpeg?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*DRxMoUVu1SXHL6BCpR8xpQ.jpeg">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*DRxMoUVu1SXHL6BCpR8xpQ.jpeg">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="34c9" id="34c9" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Maybe you’ve used Twilio before, or maybe you haven’t but you’re extremely interested in playing with programmable telephony and bringing it to your team or company. With the past success of our “Build” articles (like <a href="https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/build-a-serverless-slack-bot-in-9-minutes-with-node-js-and-stdlib-b993cfa15358" data-href="https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/build-a-serverless-slack-bot-in-9-minutes-with-node-js-and-stdlib-b993cfa15358" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" target="_blank">Build a Slack Bot in 9 Minutes</a>), we’re excited to share StdLib’s quickest article yet?—?we’re happy to introduce how you can build a Twilio Messaging Hub in only 7 Minutes with StdLib!</p>
           <p name="0dda" id="0dda" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">If you haven’t used StdLib before you’re in for a treat?—?<a href="https://stdlib.com/" data-href="https://stdlib.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">StdLib is the fastest way to ship business value via code</a>. It’s effectively a package manager for APIs that’s built upon new “serverless” architecture, meaning you never have to worry about managing servers or allocating resources for scale. Write a function, deploy, and you’re ready to go! We also have a growing ecosystem of integrations contributed by other developers that are extremely easy to plug in to.</p>
           <p name="cc7b" id="cc7b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Once you’ve created your StdLib service in <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Minute 4</strong>, you’ll get a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">README.md</code>file that shows you how to hack your Twilio + StdLib Messaging Hub to your own needs.</p>
           <h3 name="7993" id="7993" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">What You’ll Need Beforehand</h3>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="615f" id="615f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--h3">1x <a href="https://twilio.com/" data-href="https://twilio.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Twilio Account</a></li>
            <li name="e492" id="e492" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">1x Command Line Terminal</li>
            <li name="84b7" id="84b7" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li graf--trailing">7x Minutes (or 420x Seconds)</li>
           </ul>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

           <h3 name="50c3" id="50c3" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Minute 1: Create Your Twilio Phone&nbsp;Number</h3>
           <p name="626d" id="626d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">The first thing you’ll want to do to get your Stdlib + Twilio messaging hub operational is grab a new phone number for your Twilio Account. First, make sure you’re logged in to your Twilio Account at <a href="https://www.twilio.com/login" data-href="https://www.twilio.com/login" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://www.twilio.com/login</a>.</p>
           <figure name="618b" id="618b" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">

           <h3 name="656b" id="656b" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Minute 2: StdLib Account&nbsp;Setup</h3>
           <p name="383e" id="383e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">In order to create a robust messaging hub, you’ll next need to set up your <a href="https://stdlib.com/" data-href="https://stdlib.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">StdLib</a> Account. You’ll use StdLib to host your Twilio Hub using infinitely scalable “serverless” architecture from a single, maintainable codebase, and to hook into other integrations on StdLib (for example, using <a href="https://stdlib.com/utils/image" data-href="https://stdlib.com/utils/image" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">utils.image</a> to format images you receive via MMS or using <a href="https://stdlib.com/devin/income-predictor" data-href="https://stdlib.com/devin/income-predictor" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">devin.income-predictor</a> to see income ranges for the zip code associated with an incoming phone number). Simply visit <a href="https://stdlib.com" data-href="https://stdlib.com" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">https://stdlib.com</a> and click “Sign Up Free” to create your account.</p>
           <figure name="2231" id="2231" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 364px;">

             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*qCHJKBgIEyBsBJ7ecZzHBg.png" data-width="2052" data-height="1066" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*qCHJKBgIEyBsBJ7ecZzHBg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*qCHJKBgIEyBsBJ7ecZzHBg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">

           <h3 name="e113" id="e113" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Minute 3: Create a StdLib Workspace</h3>
           <p name="d9c7" id="d9c7" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3"><a href="https://medium.com/stdlibhq/stdlib-updates-node-8-0-0-platform-support-new-faaslang-function-definitions-b33ffe5633b8" data-href="https://medium.com/stdlibhq/stdlib-updates-node-8-0-0-platform-support-new-faaslang-function-definitions-b33ffe5633b8" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" target="_blank">StdLib natively runs Node.js 8.0.0 (yes, the newest version)</a> so to ensure there are no compatibility issues you’ll likely want to run it (though Node 6 and 7 will work for this example). You can install the latest version of Node from the <a href="https://nodejs.org" data-href="https://nodejs.org" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Official Node.js Website</a>. Once complete, open up your Terminal or Command Line and install the <a href="https://github.com/stdlib/lib" data-href="https://github.com/stdlib/lib" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener nofollow noopener" target="_blank">StdLib Command Line Tools</a> with the following:</p>
           <pre name="f0c1" id="f0c1" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ npm install lib.cli -g</pre>
           <p name="7885" id="7885" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">This gives you access to the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">lib</code> command for service management and execution. Next, create a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">stdlib</code> directory for your StdLib services.</p>
           <pre name="59ae" id="59ae" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ mkdir stdlib<br>$ cd stdlib<br>$ lib init</pre>
           <p name="1c45" id="1c45" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre graf--trailing">Log in using the credentials you created in the previous step. That’s it!</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="4278" class="section section--body">

           <h3 name="01f5" id="01f5" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Minute 4: StdLib Service&nbsp;Creation</h3>
           <p name="b428" id="b428" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Next you’ll create your StdLib service from the command line. We’ve created a special <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">twilio</code> template to allow you to ship a prototype of your own Twilio Hub in only a few seconds.</p>
           <pre name="31bf" id="31bf" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ lib create -t twilio</pre>
           <p name="a6d6" id="a6d6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">You’ll be asked to enter a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Service Name</code>, we recommend <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">twilio-hub</code> for the purposes of this tutorial. You’ll see some NPM packages being installed locally and your service directory being created:</p>
           <figure name="b174" id="b174" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 223px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 31.900000000000002%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*fNLziZv9uQC6bEfWHvplbg.png" data-width="810" data-height="258" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*fNLziZv9uQC6bEfWHvplbg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*fNLziZv9uQC6bEfWHvplbg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*fNLziZv9uQC6bEfWHvplbg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*fNLziZv9uQC6bEfWHvplbg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="7e04" id="7e04" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Once complete, you’ll be told to enter your service directory. Do so with the command:</p>
           <pre name="5021" id="5021" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ cd user/twilio-hub</pre>
           <p name="ff79" id="ff79" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">Where <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">user</code> is, of course, your StdLib username. (In my case, it’s <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">keith</code>.)</p>
           <figure name="0b05" id="0b05" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 292px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 41.699999999999996%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*50xp9R0MQlP4ljQOO9IEtQ.png" data-width="892" data-height="372" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*50xp9R0MQlP4ljQOO9IEtQ.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*50xp9R0MQlP4ljQOO9IEtQ.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*50xp9R0MQlP4ljQOO9IEtQ.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*50xp9R0MQlP4ljQOO9IEtQ.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="f5cc" id="f5cc" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">From here, you can try running some SMS commands (these will be the responses for <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">“more”</em> or <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">“whoami”</em> sent to your Twilio number) with:</p>
           <pre name="55c6" id="55c6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ lib .messaging.more</pre>
           <p name="967a" id="967a" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">And see the result:</p>
           <figure name="0f82" id="0f82" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 63px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 9%;"></div>
             <img class="graf-image" data-image-id="1*v-gwA2hKYp2WJ8OM0lGH3Q.png" data-width="1020" data-height="92" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*v-gwA2hKYp2WJ8OM0lGH3Q.png" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*v-gwA2hKYp2WJ8OM0lGH3Q.png">
            </div>
            <figcaption class="imageCaption">
             The SMS response to people who message your number with the text&nbsp;“more.”
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p name="b201" id="b201" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Or, alternatively, turn on debug mode with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">-d</code> to see what’s going on behind the scenes:</p>
           <pre name="d383" id="d383" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ lib .messaging.whoami -d</pre>
           <figure name="5434" id="5434" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--pre">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 161px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 23%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*DRdneqHvjE0f4DVBYTT6Kg.png" data-width="1724" data-height="396" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*DRdneqHvjE0f4DVBYTT6Kg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*DRdneqHvjE0f4DVBYTT6Kg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*DRdneqHvjE0f4DVBYTT6Kg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*DRdneqHvjE0f4DVBYTT6Kg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="88b5" id="88b5" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure graf--trailing">Since this isn’t actually being triggered by Twilio’s webhook, execution information (zipcode, city) reads as <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">undefined</code>, so this is expected.</p>
          </div>

           <h3 name="a90f" id="a90f" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"><strong class="markup--strong markup--h3-strong">Minute 5: Configure Your StdLib Environment</strong></h3>
           <p name="a627" id="a627" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">As a next step, we’ll want to make sure StdLib knows all of our Twilio Account details. To set this up properly, first open up <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">env.json</code> in the StdLib service directory you just created, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">user/twilio-hub/env.json</code> where, again, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">user</code> is your username.</p>
           <figure name="8b3c" id="8b3c" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 526px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75.1%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*89hCOaojXf-OBnLf6mHdOg.png" data-width="1222" data-height="918" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*89hCOaojXf-OBnLf6mHdOg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*89hCOaojXf-OBnLf6mHdOg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*89hCOaojXf-OBnLf6mHdOg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*89hCOaojXf-OBnLf6mHdOg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="8551" id="8551" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">You can see three different environments: <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">local</code>, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dev</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">release</code>. These are intended for different execution contexts?—?when running locally, the environment variables in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">local</code> are used, you can deploy to a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dev</code> environment in the cloud, or a production <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">release</code> environment. We generally recommend at least using a different phone number.</p>
           <p name="3373" id="3373" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Make sure, for the purposes of this tutorial, you fill in the </strong><code class="markup--code markup--p-code"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">dev</strong></code><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"> and </strong><code class="markup--code markup--p-code"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">local</strong></code><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"> variables with the same values.</strong></p>
           <p name="7112" id="7112" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">To fill in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">"STDLIB_TOKEN"</code> visit <a href="https://dashboard.stdlib.com/dashboard/" data-href="https://dashboard.stdlib.com/dashboard/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">https://dashboard.stdlib.com/dashboard/</a>, log in, click <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Library Tokens</strong> on the left, then <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Show Token</strong> to reveal your token. Copy and paste it into your environment variables.</p>
           <figure name="d6bd" id="d6bd" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 262px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 37.4%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*1jQGQVacvUaXl-96m52gcg.png" data-width="1994" data-height="746" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*1jQGQVacvUaXl-96m52gcg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*1jQGQVacvUaXl-96m52gcg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*1jQGQVacvUaXl-96m52gcg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*1jQGQVacvUaXl-96m52gcg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figcaption class="imageCaption">
             Click “Show Token” to reveal your token, then copy&nbsp;it.
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p name="4c3c" id="4c3c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Next, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">"TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID"</code>, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">"TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN"</code>, and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">"TWILIO_NUMBER"</code>?—?these are all available from your Twilio Console at <a href="https://www.twilio.com/console" data-href="https://www.twilio.com/console" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://www.twilio.com/console</a>. Copy your <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">ACCOUNT SID</strong> directly, and click the eyeball beside your <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">AUTH TOKEN</strong> to reveal it and copy it as well.</p>
           <figure name="f930" id="f930" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 291px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 41.5%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*GFcOJDQeLd6HV_yE6SvHKQ.png" data-width="1180" data-height="490" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*GFcOJDQeLd6HV_yE6SvHKQ.png">

            <figcaption class="imageCaption">
             Copy your Account SID and your Twilio Auth Token into your Environment Variables
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p name="5073" id="5073" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">To find your Twilio Phone Number you previously created, visit <a href="https://www.twilio.com/console/phone-numbers/incoming" data-href="https://www.twilio.com/console/phone-numbers/incoming" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://www.twilio.com/console/phone-numbers/incoming</a>. Click on the red, highlighted number you created in <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Minute 1</strong>.</p>

             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*YXtPmYOYwmEvNMfdgZm7Tg.png" data-width="1764" data-height="758" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*YXtPmYOYwmEvNMfdgZm7Tg.png">

              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*YXtPmYOYwmEvNMfdgZm7Tg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*YXtPmYOYwmEvNMfdgZm7Tg.png">

             Click on the Red Text to Configure Your&nbsp;Number
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p name="25aa" id="25aa" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">From the next screen, copy and paste the <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">PHONE NUMBER</strong> value in the format <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">+1234567890</code> to your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">"TWILIO_NUMBER"</code> value.</p>

Use the format <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">+1234567890</code> again (make sure it’s in quotes). Best bet is to use a personal phone number for demonstration purposes.</p>

           <h3 name="901e" id="901e" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Minute 6: Deploy and Configure Webhooks</h3>
           <p name="cbd0" id="cbd0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">You’re almost done! The very last step is to deploy your StdLib Twilio Hub (with the appropriate environment variables set above) and then configure Twilio Webhooks to point to StdLib.</p>
           <p name="3d33" id="3d33" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">To deploy your StdLib Twilio Hub in a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dev</code> environment, simply open up your command line in your service directory and type:</p>
           <pre name="c969" id="c969" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">$ lib up dev</pre>
           <p name="580c" id="580c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">You’ll see the progress of your service deploying to a development environment, and be greeted with a list of available HTTP endpoints corresponding to everything in your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">functions/</code> directory.</p>
           <figure name="bd20" id="bd20" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 182px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 25.900000000000002%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*6DB9d1R5TgFGbj83_W1viQ.png" data-width="1326" data-height="344" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*6DB9d1R5TgFGbj83_W1viQ.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*6DB9d1R5TgFGbj83_W1viQ.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*6DB9d1R5TgFGbj83_W1viQ.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*6DB9d1R5TgFGbj83_W1viQ.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="fc57" id="fc57" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Now that your service is live, go back to the Twilio Manage Numbers dashboard <a href="https://www.twilio.com/console/phone-numbers/incoming" data-href="https://www.twilio.com/console/phone-numbers/incoming" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener noopener" target="_blank">https://www.twilio.com/console/phone-numbers/incoming</a> and select your phone number again. Scroll down to <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Voice &amp; Fax</strong> first:</p>
           <figure name="d4ad" id="d4ad" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 326px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 46.6%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*QWKhEHBghyYLQz3tYTUxZQ.png" data-width="1692" data-height="788" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*QWKhEHBghyYLQz3tYTUxZQ.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*QWKhEHBghyYLQz3tYTUxZQ.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*QWKhEHBghyYLQz3tYTUxZQ.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*QWKhEHBghyYLQz3tYTUxZQ.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figcaption class="imageCaption">
             Enter in your “voice” endpoint to Voice &amp;&nbsp;Fax
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p name="2ad3" id="2ad3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">On this form, beside <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">A CALL COMES IN</strong>, make sure <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Webhook</strong> is selected in the dropdown and use the value <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">https://&lt;user&gt;.lib.id/twilio-hub@dev/voice/</code> (where <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">&lt;user&gt;</code> is of course, your username). Note that the hostname <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">lib.id</code> is our functions gateway, where all of your services and functions will be deployed to.</p>
           <p name="ebc2" id="ebc2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Next, scroll down to <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Messaging</strong> and enter in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">https://&lt;user&gt;.lib.id/twilio-hub@dev/messaging/</code> in the <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">A MESSAGE COMES IN</strong> Webhook handler.</p>
           <figure name="fd5b" id="fd5b" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 230px;">

             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*BmytJ5Mj_CK23gmxl04XXw.png" data-width="1750" data-height="576" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*BmytJ5Mj_CK23gmxl04XXw.png">

              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*BmytJ5Mj_CK23gmxl04XXw.png">

             </div>
            </div>
            <figcaption class="imageCaption">
             Enter in your Messaging Handler details, and hit&nbsp;
             <strong class="markup--strong markup--figure-strong">Save</strong>

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="6bee" id="6bee" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Minute 7: Add Verified Phone&nbsp;Numbers</h3>
           <p name="65a1" id="65a1" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">If this is your first time signing up with Twilio, you’ll be using a trial account. Trial accounts have limitations on numbers they can send messages to or forward calls from. To make sure your Twilio Messaging Hub on StdLib works as you expect it, use the <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">verified phone numbers</strong> list to add any phone numbers that you want to forward calls or send messages to.</p>
           <p name="449c" id="449c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://twilio.com/user/account/phone-numbers/verified." data-href="https://twilio.com/user/account/phone-numbers/verified." class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">https://twilio.com/user/account/phone-numbers/verified</a></p>
           <figure name="4cd4" id="4cd4" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 264px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 37.7%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*b6Ne5iVu0wwEBACwJEfsdg.png" data-width="1946" data-height="734" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*b6Ne5iVu0wwEBACwJEfsdg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*b6Ne5iVu0wwEBACwJEfsdg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*b6Ne5iVu0wwEBACwJEfsdg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*b6Ne5iVu0wwEBACwJEfsdg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="7e64" id="7e64" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure graf--trailing">By default, the phone number you registered your account with should already be listed here.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="31bb" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="d119" id="d119" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">That’s It!</h3>
           <p name="4f23" id="4f23" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Your Twilio Messaging Hub on StdLib is live! You can now send SMS messages to your Twilio Number to receive an automated response and make calls to your number to have them forwarded. <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">If you’re using a Twilio trial account, make sure you’ve added verified numbers in Minute 7. </strong>Otherwise, you’re good to go!</p>
           <figure name="bf90" id="bf90" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 1245px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 177.89999999999998%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*6UyblhY2t--1mxYegHoWQg.png" data-width="750" data-height="1334" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*6UyblhY2t--1mxYegHoWQg.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*6UyblhY2t--1mxYegHoWQg.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*6UyblhY2t--1mxYegHoWQg.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*6UyblhY2t--1mxYegHoWQg.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figcaption class="imageCaption">
             A Twilio Bot Interaction using&nbsp;StdLib
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p name="69ed" id="69ed" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">You can modify the behavior of your SMS Bot by visiting the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">/functions/messaging/</code> directory in your StdLib service. The default responses are are to “whoami” and “more.” This messaging hub also handles MMS (media, picture) uploads.</p>
           <h4 name="5e57" id="5e57" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Gotchas and Production Releases</h4>
           <p name="442e" id="442e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">If at any point you lose track of your StdLib username or what your webhook callbacks should be, they’re listed when you deploy a service with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">$ lib up dev</code>.</p>
           <p name="50de" id="50de" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">If you’re not getting the expected responses when you play, Twilio has an amazing debugger at <a href="https://www.twilio.com/console/dev-tools/debugger" data-href="https://www.twilio.com/console/dev-tools/debugger" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener noopener" target="_blank">https://www.twilio.com/console/dev-tools/debugger</a>.</p>
           <p name="617c" id="617c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing">To ship a bot / messaging hub to production, we recommend using a different phone number. Configure your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">release</code> environment variables in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">env.json</code> to the appropriate settings, set your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">version</code> in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">package.json</code> to <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">1.0.0</code> (or whatever you’d like, really), ship a release with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">$ lib release</code> and then you can use <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">https://&lt;user&gt;.lib.id/twilio-hub@1.0.0/voice/</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">https://&lt;user&gt;.lib.id/twilio-hub@1.0.0/messaging/</code> as your voice and messaging endpoints for your production phone number.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="1298" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="5d10" id="5d10" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading">Thank You!</h3>
           <p name="65da" id="65da" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3 graf--trailing">If you’d like to keep track of future StdLib updates and more Twilio fun, please follow us on Twitter at <a href="https://twitter.com/StdLibHQ" data-href="https://twitter.com/StdLibHQ" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">@StdLibHQ?</a>—?or you can follow me, specifically at <a href="https://twitter.com/keithwhor" data-href="https://twitter.com/keithwhor" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">@keithwhor.</a> Thanks for reading!</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
